// Protect Geist code blocks from 1Password DOM flattening
(function() {
  const codeBlockSnapshots = new WeakMap();
  let isRestoring = false;

  function saveSnapshot(codeElement) {
    if (!codeBlockSnapshots.has(codeElement)) {
      codeBlockSnapshots.set(codeElement, codeElement.cloneNode(true));
    }
  }

  function checkAndRestore(codeElement) {
    if (isRestoring) return;

    // Check if our specific structure was flattened
    const hasOurStructure = codeElement.querySelector('[data-geist-code-block-line]');
    const snapshot = codeBlockSnapshots.get(codeElement);

    if (!hasOurStructure && snapshot && snapshot.querySelector('[data-geist-code-block-line]')) {
      // Our structure was destroyed (likely by 1Password), restore it
      isRestoring = true;
      codeElement.innerHTML = snapshot.innerHTML;
      isRestoring = false;
    }
  }

  function initializeCodeBlocks() {
    document.querySelectorAll('code[data-geist-code-block]').forEach(saveSnapshot);
  }

  // Single global observer for all code blocks
  const globalObserver = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
    if (isRestoring) return;

    mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
      // Check if new code blocks were added
      mutation.addedNodes.forEach(function(node) {
        if (node.nodeType === 1) {
          if (node.matches && node.matches('code[data-geist-code-block]')) {
            saveSnapshot(node);
          } else if (node.querySelectorAll) {
            node.querySelectorAll('code[data-geist-code-block]').forEach(saveSnapshot);
          }
        }
      });

      // Check if existing code blocks were modified
      var target = mutation.target;
      if (target.nodeType === 1) {
        // Check if the target itself is a protected code block
        if (target.matches && target.matches('code[data-geist-code-block]')) {
          checkAndRestore(target);
        }
        // Check if the target contains protected code blocks
        else if (target.closest && target.closest('code[data-geist-code-block]')) {
          checkAndRestore(target.closest('code[data-geist-code-block]'));
        }
      }
    });
  });

  // Initialize existing code blocks and start observing
  function init() {
    initializeCodeBlocks();
    globalObserver.observe(document.documentElement, {
      childList: true,
      subtree: true,
      characterData: true
    });
  }

  // Run immediately and after DOM is ready
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
  } else {
    init();
  }
})();

14H7.75C7.61193 14 7.5 13.8881 7.5 13.75V6.25Z" fill="currentColor"/></svg><span class="hidden sm:inline-block">Copy markdown</span></div></span></button></div></div><h1 id="agents" data-docs-heading=""><a href="#agents">Agents<span><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" height="0.7em" width="0.7em">
  <g stroke-width="1.2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor">
    <path fill="none" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-miterlimit="10" d="M8.995,7.005 L8.995,7.005c1.374,1.374,1.374,3.601,0,4.975l-1.99,1.99c-1.374,1.374-3.601,1.374-4.975,0l0,0c-1.374-1.374-1.374-3.601,0-4.975 l1.748-1.698"></path>
    <path fill="none" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-miterlimit="10" d="M7.005,8.995 L7.005,8.995c-1.374-1.374-1.374-3.601,0-4.975l1.99-1.99c1.374-1.374,3.601-1.374,4.975,0l0,0c1.374,1.374,1.374,3.601,0,4.975 l-1.748,1.698"></path>
  </g>
</svg></span></a></h1>
<p>Agents are <strong>large language models (LLMs)</strong> that use <strong>tools</strong> in a <strong>loop</strong> to accomplish tasks.</p>
<p>These components work together:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>LLMs</strong> process input and decide the next action</li>
<li><strong>Tools</strong> extend capabilities beyond text generation (reading files, calling APIs, writing to databases)</li>
<li><strong>Loop</strong> orchestrates execution through:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li><strong>Context management</strong> - Maintaining conversation history and deciding what the model sees (input) at each step</li>
<li><strong>Stopping conditions</strong> - Determining when the loop (task) is complete</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="toolloopagent-class" data-docs-heading=""><a href="#toolloopagent-class">ToolLoopAgent Class<span><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" height="0.7em" width="0.7em">
  <g stroke-width="1.2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor">
    <path fill="none" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-miterlimit="10" d="M8.995,7.005 L8.995,7.005c1.374,1.374,1.374,3.601,0,4.975l-1.99,1.99c-1.374,1.374-3.601,1.374-4.975,0l0,0c-1.374-1.374-1.374-3.601,0-4.975 l1.748-1.698"></path>
    <path fill="none" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-miterlimit="10" d="M7.005,8.995 L7.005,8.995c-1.374-1.374-1.374-3.601,0-4.975l1.99-1.99c1.374-1.374,3.601-1.374,4.975,0l0,0c1.374,1.374,1.374,3.601,0,4.975 l-1.748,1.698"></path>
  </g>
</svg></span></a></h2>
<p>The ToolLoopAgent class handles these three components. Here&#x27;s an agent that uses multiple tools in a loop to accomplish a task:</p>

off"><button aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" type="button" aria-label="Add line anchor to the URL" class="code-block-module__VkAzma__lineNumber">28</button><div class="token-line"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span><span class="token plain"></span></div></div><div class="line" data-geist-code-block-line="true" id="C66a87c24-L29" data-highlighted="false" style="font-feature-settings:&quot;liga&quot; off"><button aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" type="button" aria-label="Add line anchor to the URL" class="code-block-module__VkAzma__lineNumber">29</button><div class="token-line"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block">
</span></div></div><div class="line" data-geist-code-block-line="true" id="C66a87c24-L30" data-highlighted="false" style="font-feature-settings:&quot;liga&quot; off"><button aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" type="button" aria-label="Add line anchor to the URL" class="code-block-module__VkAzma__lineNumber">30</button><div class="token-line"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword">const</span><span class="token plain"> result </span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token keyword">await</span><span class="token plain"> weatherAgent</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">generate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token plain"></span></div></div><div class="line" data-geist-code-block-line="true" id="C66a87c24-L31" data-highlighted="false" style="font-feature-settings:&quot;liga&quot; off"><button aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" type="button" aria-label="Add line anchor to the URL" class="code-block-module__VkAzma__lineNumber">31</button><div class="token-line"><span class="token plain">  prompt</span><span class="token operator">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string">&#x27;What is the weather in San Francisco in celsius?&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token plain"></span></div></div><div class="line" data-geist-code-block-line="true" id="C66a87c24-L32" data-highlighted="false" style="font-feature-settings:&quot;liga&quot; off"><button aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" type="button" aria-label="Add line anchor to the URL" class="code-block-module__VkAzma__lineNumber">32</button><div class="token-line"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span><span class="token plain"></span></div></div><div class="line" data-geist-code-block-line="true" id="C66a87c24-L33" data-highlighted="false" style="font-feature-settings:&quot;liga&quot; off"><button aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" type="button" aria-label="Add line anchor to the URL" class="code-block-module__VkAzma__lineNumber">33</button><div class="token-line"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block">
</span></div></div><div class="line" data-geist-code-block-line="true" id="C66a87c24-L34" data-highlighted="false" style="font-feature-settings:&quot;liga&quot; off"><button aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" type="button" aria-label="Add line anchor to the URL" class="code-block-module__VkAzma__lineNumber">34</button><div class="token-line"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token plain">result</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token plain">text</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment">// agent&#x27;s final answer</span><span class="token plain"></span></div></div><div class="line" data-geist-code-block-line="true" id="C66a87c24-L35" data-highlighted="false" style="font-feature-settings:&quot;liga&quot; off"><button aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" type="button" aria-label="Add line anchor to the URL" class="code-block-module__VkAzma__lineNumber">35</button><div class="token-line"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token builtin">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token plain">result</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token plain">steps</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment">// steps taken by the agent</span></div></div></code></pre></div></div></div>
<p>The agent automatically:</p>
<ol>
<li>Calls the <code>weather</code> tool to get the temperature in Fahrenheit</li>
<li>Calls <code>convertFahrenheitToCelsius</code> to convert it</li>
<li>Generates a final text response with the result</li>
</ol>
<p>The ToolLoopAgent handles the loop, context management, and stopping conditions.</p>
<h2 id="why-use-the-toolloopagent" data-docs-heading=""><a href="#why-use-the-toolloopagent">Why Use the ToolLoopAgent?<span><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" height="0.7em" width="0.7em">
  <g stroke-width="1.2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor">
    <path fill="none" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-miterlimit="10" d="M8.995,7.005 L8.995,7.005c1.374,1.374,1.374,3.601,0,4.975l-1.99,1.99c-1.374,1.374-3.601,1.374-4.975,0l0,0c-1.374-1.374-1.374-3.601,0-4.975 l1.748-1.698"></path>
    <path fill="none" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-miterlimit="10" d="M7.005,8.995 L7.005,8.995c-1.374-1.374-1.374-3.601,0-4.975l1.99-1.99c1.374-1.374,3.601-1.374,4.975,0l0,0c1.374,1.374,1.374,3.601,0,4.975 l-1.748,1.698"></path>
  </g>
</svg></span></a></h2>
<p>The ToolLoopAgent is the recommended approach for building agents with the AI SDK because it:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Reduces boilerplate</strong> - Manages loops and message arrays</li>
<li><strong>Improves reusability</strong> - Define once, use throughout your application</li>
<li><strong>Simplifies maintenance</strong> - Single place to update agent configuration</li>
</ul>
<p>For most use cases, start with the ToolLoopAgent. Use core functions (<code>generateText</code>, <code>streamText</code>) when you need explicit control over each step for complex structured workflows.</p>
<h2 id="structured-workflows" data-docs-heading=""><a href="#structured-workflows">Structured Workflows<span><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" height="0.7em" width="0.7em">
  <g stroke-width="1.2" fill="none" stroke="currentColor">
    <path fill="none" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-miterlimit="10" d="M8.995,7.005 L8.995,7.005c1.374,1.374,1.374,3.601,0,4.975l-1.99,1.99c-1.374,1.374-3.601,1.374-4.975,0l0,0c-1.374-1.374-1.374-3.601,0-4.975 l1.748-1.698"></path>
    <path fill="none" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-miterlimit="10" d="M7.005,8.995 L7.005,8.995c-1.374-1.374-1.374-3.601,0-4.975l1.99-1.99c1.374-1.374,3.601-1.374,4.975,0l0,0c1.374,1.374,1.374,3.601,0,4.975 l-1.748,1.698"></path>
  </g>
</svg></span></a></h2>
<p>Agents are flexible and powerful, but non-deterministic. When you need reliable, repeatable outcomes with explicit control flow, use core functions with structured workflow patterns combining:</p>
<ul>
<li>Conditional statements for explicit branching</li>
<li>Standard functions for reusable logic</li>
<li>Error handling for robustness</li>
<li>Explicit control flow for predictability</li>
</ul>
<p><a href="/docs/agents/workflows">Explore workflow patterns</a> to learn more about building structured, reliable systems.</p>

    <path fill="none" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-miterlimit="10" d="M7.005,8.995 L7.005,8.995c-1.374-1.374-1.374-3.601,0-4.975l1.99-1.99c1.374-1.374,3.601-1.374,4.975,0l0,0c1.374,1.374,1.374,3.601,0,4.975 l-1.748,1.698"></path>
  </g>

Agents\n\nAgents are **large language models (LLMs)** that use **tools** in a **loop** to accomplish tasks.\n\nThese components work together:\n\n- **LLMs** process input and decide the next action\n- **Tools** extend capabilities beyond text generation (reading files, calling APIs, writing to databases)\n- **Loop** orchestrates execution through:\n  - **Context management** - Maintaining conversation history and deciding what the model sees (input) at each step\n  - **Stopping conditions** - Determining when the loop (task) is complete\n\n## ToolLoopAgent Class\n\nThe ToolLoopAgent class handles these three components. Here's an agent that uses multiple tools in a loop to accomplish a task:\n\n```ts\nimport { ToolLoopAgent, tool } from 'ai';\n__PROVIDER_IMPORT__;\nimport { z } from 'zod';\n\nconst weatherAgent = new ToolLoopAgent({\n  model: __MODEL__,\n  tools: {\n    weather: tool({\n      description: 'Get the weather in a location (in Fahrenheit)',\n      inputSchema: z.object({\n        location: z.string().describe('The location to get the weather for'),\n      }),\n      execute: async ({ location }) =\u003e ({\n        location,\n        temperature: 72 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 21) - 10,\n      }),\n    }),\n    convertFahrenheitToCelsius: tool({\n      description: 'Convert temperature from Fahrenheit to Celsius',\n      inputSchema: z.object({\n        temperature: z.number().describe('Temperature in Fahrenheit'),\n      }),\n      execute: async ({ temperature }) =\u003e {\n        const celsius = Math.round((temperature - 32) * (5 / 9));\n        return { celsius };\n      },\n    }),\n  },\n});\n\nconst result = await weatherAgent.generate({\n  prompt: 'What is the weather in San Francisco in celsius?',\n});\n\nconsole.log(result.text); // agent's final answer\nconsole.log(result.steps); // steps taken by the agent\n```\n\nThe agent automatically:\n\n1. Calls the `weather` tool to get the temperature in Fahrenheit\n2. Calls `convertFahrenheitToCelsius` to convert it\n3. Generates a final text response with the result\n\nThe ToolLoopAgent handles the loop, context management, and stopping conditions.\n\n## Why Use the ToolLoopAgent?\n\nThe ToolLoopAgent is the recommended approach for building agents with the AI SDK because it:\n\n- **Reduces boilerplate** - Manages loops and message arrays\n- **Improves reusability** - Define once, use throughout your application\n- **Simplifies maintenance** - Single place to update agent configuration\n\nFor most use cases, start with the ToolLoopAgent. Use core functions (`generateText`, `streamText`) when you need explicit control over each step for complex structured workflows.\n\n## Structured Workflows\n\nAgents are flexible and powerful, but non-deterministic. When you need reliable, repeatable outcomes with explicit control flow, use core functions with structured workflow patterns combining:\n\n- Conditional statements for explicit branching\n- Standard functions for reusable logic\n- Error handling for robustness\n- Explicit control flow for predictability\n\n[Explore workflow patterns](/docs/agents/workflows) to learn more about building structured, reliable systems.\n\n## Next Steps\n\n- **[Building Agents](/docs/agents/building-agents)** - Guide to creating agents with the ToolLoopAgent\n- **[Workflow Patterns](/docs/agents/workflows)** - Structured patterns using core functions for complex workflows\n- **[Loop Control](/docs/agents/loop-control)** - Execution control with stopWhen and prepareStep\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"1e:[\"$\",\"$L32\",null,{\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L33\",null,{\"containerAttr\":\"data-docs-container\",\"itemAttr\":\"data-docs-heading\",\"children\":[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"flex Here's an agent that uses multiple tools in a loop to accomplish a task:\n\n```ts\nimport { ToolLoopAgent, tool } from 'ai';\n__PROVIDER_IMPORT__;\nimport { z } from 'zod';\n\nconst weatherAgent = new ToolLoopAgent({\nmodel: __MODEL__,\ntools: {\nweather: tool({\ndescription: 'Get the weather in a location (in Fahrenheit)',\ninputSchema: z.object({\nlocation: z.string().describe('The location to get the weather for'),\n}),\nexecute: async ({ location }) =\u003e ({\nlocation,\ntemperature: 72 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 21) - 10,\n}),\n}),\nconvertFahrenheitToCelsius: tool({\ndescription: 'Convert temperature from Fahrenheit to Celsius',\ninputSchema: z.object({\ntemperature: z.number().describe('Temperature in Fahrenheit'),\n}),\nexecute: async ({ temperature }) =\u003e {\nconst celsius = Math.round((temperature - 32) * (5 / 9));\nreturn { celsius };\n},\n}),\n},\n});\n\nconst result = await weatherAgent.generate({\nprompt: 'What is the weather in San Francisco in celsius?',\n});\n\nconsole.log(result.text); // agent's final answer\nconsole.log(result.steps); // steps taken by the agent\n```\n\nThe agent automatically:\n\n1. Calls the `weather` tool to get the temperature in Fahrenheit\n2. Calls `convertFahrenheitToCelsius` to convert it\n3. Generates a final text response with the result\n\nThe ToolLoopAgent handles the loop, context management, and stopping conditions."])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"39:[\"$\",\"$L3c\",null,{\"tableOfContents\":[{\"level\":1,\"title\":\"Agents\",\"slug\":\"agents\",\"content\":\"Agents are **large language models (LLMs)** that use **tools** in a **loop** to accomplish tasks.\\n\\nThese components work together:\\n\\n- **LLMs** process input and decide the next action\\n- **Tools** extend capabilities beyond text generation (reading files, calling APIs, writing to databases)\\n- **Loop** orchestrates execution through:\\n- **Context management** - Maintaining conversation history and deciding what the model sees (input) at each step\\n- **Stopping conditions** - Determining when the loop (task) is complete\",\"children\":[{\"level\":2,\"title\":\"ToolLoopAgent Class\",\"slug\":\"toolloopagent-class\",\"content\":\"$3d\",\"children\":[]},{\"level\":2,\"title\":\"Why Use the ToolLoopAgent?\",\"slug\":\"why-use-the-toolloopagent\",\"content\":\"The ToolLoopAgent is the recommended approach for building agents with the AI SDK because it:\\n\\n- **Reduces boilerplate** - Manages loops and message arrays\\n- **Improves reusability** - Define once, use throughout your application\\n- **Simplifies maintenance** - Single place to update agent configuration\\n\\nFor most use cases, start with the ToolLoopAgent. Use core functions (`generateText`, `streamText`) when you need explicit control over each step for complex structured workflows.\",\"children\":[]},{\"level\":2,\"title\":\"Structured Workflows\",\"slug\":\"structured-workflows\",\"content\":\"Agents are flexible and powerful, but non-deterministic. When you need reliable, repeatable outcomes with explicit control flow, use core functions with structured workflow patterns combining:\\n\\n- Conditional statements for explicit branching\\n- Standard functions for reusable logic\\n- Error handling for robustness\\n- Explicit control flow for predictability\\n\\n[Explore workflow patterns](/docs/agents/workflows) to learn more about building structured, reliable systems.\",\"children\":[]},{\"level\":2,\"title\":\"Next Steps\",\"slug\":\"next-steps\",\"content\":\"- **[Building Agents](/docs/agents/building-agents)** - Guide to { ToolLoopAgent, tool } from 'ai';\n__PROVIDER_IMPORT__;\nimport { z } from 'zod';\n\nconst weatherAgent = new ToolLoopAgent({\n  model: __MODEL__,\n  tools: {\n    weather: tool({\n      description: 'Get the weather in a location (in Fahrenheit)',\n      inputSchema: z.object({\n        location: z.string().describe('The location to get the weather for'),\n      }),\n      execute: async ({ location }) =\u003e ({\n        location,\n        temperature: 72 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 21) - 10,\n      }),\n    }),\n    convertFahrenheitToCelsius: tool({\n      description: 'Convert temperature from Fahrenheit to Celsius',\n      inputSchema: z.object({\n        temperature: z.number().describe('Temperature in Fahrenheit'),\n      }),\n      execute: async ({ temperature }) =\u003e {\n        const celsius = Math.round((temperature - 32) * (5 / 9));\n        return { celsius };\n      },\n    }),\n  },\n});\n\nconst result = await weatherAgent.generate({\n  prompt: 'What is the weather in San Francisco in celsius?',\n});\n\nconsole.log(result.text); // agent's final answer\nconsole.log(result.steps); // steps taken by the agent\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"37:[[\"$\",\"h1\",null,{\"id\":\"agents\",\"data-docs-heading\":\"\",\"children\":[\"$\",\"a\",null,{\"href\":\"#agents\",\"children\":[\"Agents\",[\"$\",\"span\",null,{\"children\":[\"$\",\"svg\",null,{\"viewBox\":\"0
